 ise nawabon ke shahar ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 Sarrafa Chowk, Moti Masjid, Taj-ul Masjid, Gauhar Mahal and more than one architectural specimen reflect the rich heritage and culture of the city
 taj ul masjid desh kii apni tarah kii sabase badi masjid he, ise nawab shah jahaan begum ne banvaanaa shuru kiya lekin paise kii kami kii vajah se deree hoti gai aakhir main jaakar ye 1971 main puri ho pai
 At the same time, the grand Moti Masjid was built inspired by Jama Masjid of Delhi
 1860 main kudasia begum kii beti sikandar jahaan ne ise banwaaya
 Moti Masjid built by Sikandar Jahan is a wonderful blend of Islamic and French architecture

 It is a splendid example of Mughal and Hindu architectural styles
 yah pehla mahal tha, jise bhopal ke shaskaon ne banwaaya tha

 " unhone kaha, "aane vaale varshon main bhi yahi rujhaan bana rahegaa kyonki nae nijee bank ke pravesh se udyog kaa vistaar hoga
 " pichley saal sarkari bainkon ne kareeb 63 hajaar nai niyuktiyaan kii thi
 The State Bank of India alone had 20 thousand clerks and 1,200 officers reinstated
 anya sarkari bainkon main 22 hajaar adhikariyon or 20 hajaar lipic kii bahaali hui thi
 In addition, in the current financial year, public sector banks are going to add about 8,000 additional branches to their existing network
 isse bhi kaarobaar badhegaa or nai naukariyon ke avasar badhenge
 The comments nijee bank, kshetreey gramin bank or videshi bank bhi vartmaan vitt varsh main shakhaon kii sankhya badhayenge
 Apart from this, if the Reserve Bank of India issues new licenses at the end of the current financial year, then the path of entry of new private banks will be ready in the next financial year
 isse kareeb ek lakh or naukariyon ke avasar taiyaar honge
 The study conducted by the Associated Chambers of Commerce and Industry (assocham) stated that new jobs would be created due to expansion of branches, new banks and retirement of old personnel

 Apart from this, more than 50 thousand jobs will be provided in 20 private banks, regional rural banks and foreign banks in the same period
 " He said, "the same trend will continue in the coming years as the entry of new private bank will expand the industry
" " Last year, around 63 thousand new appointments were made by state-run banks
